! Title: uBlock Search Filters ‚Äì General & GitHub/NPM Copycats
! Description: This filter list blocks spam, duplicate, or low-quality search results across major search engines.
! Homepage: https://github.com/rxreborn/ubo-static-blacklist
! Forums: https://github.com/rxreborn/ubo-static-blacklist/issues
! Advanced Setting: Ensure `allowGenericProceduralFilters` is enabled: https://github.com/gorhill/uBlock/wiki/Advanced-settings#allowgenericproceduralfilters
! Last Updated: 2025-02-07
! - Generated by letsblock.it: https://github.com/letsblockit/letsblockit (Discontinued)
!
! ==========================
! üåç Affected Search Engines:
! ==========================
! - Google
! - DuckDuckGo
! - Startpage
!
! ==========================
! üõë What This Filter Blocks:
! ==========================
! - Pinterest, Softonic, and other spammy/unwanted domains in search results.
! - Duplicate or misleading repositories copied from GitHub.
! - Low-value NPM package mirrors.
! - Stack Overflow clone sites that duplicate answers without adding value.
! - Other general spammy domains that degrade search result quality.
!
! ==========================
! üìú Sources and License:
! ==========================
! - GitHub copycats: https://github.com/quenhus/uBlock-Origin-dev-filter/blob/main/data/github_copycats.txt
! - NPM package mirrors: https://github.com/quenhus/uBlock-Origin-dev-filter/blob/main/data/npm_copycats.txt
! - Stack Overflow clones: https://github.com/quenhus/uBlock-Origin-dev-filter/blob/main/data/stackoverflow_copycats.txt
! - License: https://github.com/quenhus/uBlock-Origin-dev-filter/blob/main/LICENSE

www.google.*##.g:has(a[href*=".pinterest."])
www.google.*##a[href*=".pinterest."]:upward(1)
duckduckgo.com##ol.react-results--main a[href*=".pinterest."]:upward(article)
duckduckgo.com##.tile-wrap a[href*=".pinterest."]:upward(.tile)
startpage.com##.w-gl__result:has(a[href*=".pinterest."])
startpage.com##.image-container:has(div.image-quick-details span:has-text(.pinterest.))
www.google.*##.g:has(a[href*=".softonic."])
www.google.*##a[href*=".softonic."]:upward(1)
duckduckgo.com##ol.react-results--main a[href*=".softonic."]:upward(article)
duckduckgo.com##.tile-wrap a[href*=".softonic."]:upward(.tile)
startpage.com##.w-gl__result:has(a[href*=".softonic."])
startpage.com##.image-container:has(div.image-quick-details span:has-text(.softonic.))
